The Gazette of the Democratic Socialist Republic of  Sri Lanka
IMPORTANT  NOTICE  REGARDING  ACCEPTANCE  OF  NOTICES
FOR  PUBLICATION  IN  THE  WEEKLY  “GAZETTE”
ATTENTION is drawn to the Notification appearing in the 1st week of every month, regarding the latest dates and times of accept ance
of Notices for publication in the weekly Gazettes, at the end of every weekly Gazette of Democratic Socialist Republic of Sri Lanka.
All Notices to be published in the weekly Gazettes  shall close at 12.00 noon of each Friday, two weeks before the date of
publication. All Government Departments, Corporations, Boards, etc. are hereby advised that Notifications fixing closing dates and times
of applications in respect of Post-vacancies, Examinations, Tender Notices and dates and times of Auction Sales, etc. should be  prepared
by giving adequate time both from the date of despatch of notices to Govt. Press and from the date of publication, thereby enab ling those
interested in the contents of such notices to actively and positively participate please note that inquiries and complaints mad e in respect
of corrections pertaining to notification will not be entertained after three months  from the date of publication.
All Notices to be published in the weekly Gazette should reach Government Press two weeks before the date of publication i.e.
Notices for publication in the weekly Gazette of 09th September, 2016 should reach Government Press on or before 12.00 noon on 26th
August, 2016.
Electronic Transactions Act, No. 19 of 2006 - Section 9
“Where any Act or Enactment provides that any proclamation, rule, regulation, order , by-law, notification or other matter shall
be published in the Gazette, then such requirement shall be deemed to have been satisfied if such rule, regulation, order, by-l aw,
notification or other matter is published in an electronic form of the Gazette.”.
B. K. S. R
A VINDRA,
 Government Printer ( Acting ).
Department of Govt. Printing,
Colombo 08,
21st June, 2016.
This Gazette can be downloaded from www.documents.gov.lk

of the Democratic Socialist Republic of Sri Lanka of June 03, 2016.

Posts – Vacant
MORATUWA  MUNICIPAL  COUNCIL
APPLICATIONS are called for the under mentioned vacant posts in the Moratuwa Municipal Council, from applicants who
possess qualifications mentioned in this notification, and who are permanent residents in the Western Province.
Serial Designation Salary Salary Educational and Other Qualifications
No. Code Scale
01 Driver - Grade III PL3-2016 Rs. 25,790 - 10x270- (i) Should have passed G .C.E. (O/L)
10x300 - 10x330 Examination in not more than two
12x350-  Rs. 38,990/- sittings in 06 subjects with two credit passes
including Sinhala/ Tamil Language, (should
have passed at least 05 subjects in one sitting)
Professional Qualifications  :
(ii) Should have obtained a Driving License for
Motor Vehicles issued by the Commissioner
General of Motor traffic to drive private/ rented
out vehicles and station wagons of less than
the tare of 24cwt. Should have obtained
minimum of  "C" and "C1" class vehicle license
or "B" class new Driving License according
to new Driving License three (03) years before
the date of appointment.
(iii) Should have a good knowledge of Road
Regulation Code.
(iv) Should have experience of at least 03 years as
a driver (should confirm the experience by a
certificate)
(v) Minimum height should be 5 ft.
(vi) Should be physically fit to work during day
and night, and should have a sound vision.
Should be confirmed by a Medical certificate
issued by a Government Medical Officer.

Conditions of Recruitment  :
(i) Applicant should be a citizen of Sri Lanka.
(ii) Applicant should be a permanent resident in the
Western Province during the preceding three years
on the date of accepting applications.
(iii) Applicants should be not below 18 years of age
and not over 45 years as at the closing date of
applications.
(iv) Applicant should po sses a sound character and in
good health.
(v) Suitable candidates will be selected by a proper
interview on the requirements of service.
(vi) Applicant should not be a person, who had been
convicted in a Court of Law or a person who has
been punished.
(vii) The Commissioner of the Moratuwa Municipal
Council reserves the rights to delay, change or to
cancel this recruitment, either after calling
applications, or in the interim period.
(viii) Al requirements required for the appointment to
this post should be fulfilled in all aspects on the
date of the application calling Notice/ Gazette
Notice.
Conditions of Service  :
1. This post is permanent and pensionable. Selected
employees should Contribute to the W.&.O.P.
Fund.
2 . The permanent appointment is subject to a
probationary period of 03 years.
3. Appointees are bound to adhere to the Constitution
of the Democratic Socialist Republic of Sri Lanka,
Establishments Code, and Financial Regulations and
to orders from time to time issued by the Government
and Western Provincial Council.
How to send Applications :
1. Applicants should prepare their application in a A4
Size paper as shown in the specimen attached using
both sides of the paper and should be sent under
registered post addressed to Municipal
Commissioner, Municipal Council, Moratuwa to
reach on or before 20.09.2016. The name of the post
applied for should be mentioned in the application
and on the top left hand corner of the envelop. Late
applications will be rejected.
2. Photocopies of the following Certificates should
be sent along with the application :
 Birth Certificate.
 Educational Certificates.
 Certificate in respect of residence issued by
Grama Niladhari countersigned by the Divisional
Secretary.
 Two character certificates obtained recently.
(One from GS).
 A Police Report.
M.M.C.K.K. M
ANNAPPERUMA,
Municipal Commissioner,
Municipal Councils,
Moratuwa.
At the Moratuwa Municipal Council,
03rd August, 2016.

Local Government Notifications
DEPARTMENT  OF  LOCAL  GOVERNMENT
BY virtue of power vested in Pradeshiya Sabhas Under Sub-section (1) of Section 134 of Pradeshiya Sabha Act, No. 15 of
1987, the Mahanuwara Kadawath Sathara and Gangawata Korale Pradeshiya Sabha has decided under mentioned Resolution
No. 06.05, relating the declaration of Developed Areas, I do hereby notify to the General Public that I have authorized the
under mentioned Resolution by virtue of power vested in me under the said Act.
D. VATHSALA MARAMBAGE,
Assistant Commissioner of Local Government,
Kandy District.
Office of the Assistant Commissioner of
Local Government,
Kandy.
05th July, 2016.
Resolution No. 06.05. Dated 21.06.2016
According to the Resolution No. 06.II, dated 21.05.2012, as the entire Administrative Areas of Mahanuwara Kadawath
Sathara and Gangawata Korale Pradeshiya Sabha declared as developed, and published in the Gazette Notification  on
28.11.2014, all the areas which are not coming under Assessment Tax Scheme, located in either said of the roads mentioned
in the following Schedules I,II,III,IV ,V and VI are declared as developed areas by the Resolution adopted unanimously at the
General Session of the Council.

MUNICIPAL  COUNCIL - KALMUNAI
Notice under Section 7(2) of the Butchers Ordinance
NOTICE is hereby given under Section 7(2) of the Butchers Ordinance that Mr. Kalentharsha Hilmy of No. 103, Veliveriyan
Village, EFAD House Scheme, Sainthamaruthu - 16 has made an application to obtain a Butchers License under the Butchers
Ordinance (Chapter 272) to carry on the trade of a Butchers at a premises Land belong to the Masjidhul Hijra Karaivahu
Tsunami Resettlement Village, Sainthamaruthu.
If any person residing within the administrative area of the Kalmunai Municipal Council wishes to object the issue
of a Butchers License to the said person, he shall submit his objection in writing and in duplicate stating the reasons for such
objection, within a period of fourteen days from the date of publication this notice in the Gazette.
J. L
IYAKATH ALI,
Commissioner,
Municipal Council, Kalmunai.

DELFT  PRADESHIYA  SABHA
Declaration of Names and Details of Roads
IN terms of Section 24 of Pradeshiya Sabha Act, No. 15 of 1987 as per the decision (administrative order) No. 18 dated
14.07.2016 of Delft Pradeshiya Sabha in Jaffna District, by virtue if powers vested in Delft Pradeshiya Sabha as per Pradeshiya
Sabha Act roads under mentioned Schedule published as the roads belong to Delft Pradeshiya Sabha.
It is hereby notice that un terms of Section 24(2) of Pradeshiya Sabha Act, No. 15 of 1987 if anyone is to be the owner
of the land of the roads of which are identified by Delft Pradeshiya Sabha shall raise his or her objections to me with the
provable documents within one month from the date of this notice published Gazette notice with one month prior notice to
Delft Pradeshiya Sabha to establish his or her ownership.
S
OMALINGAM THAMBIRASA,
Secretary,
Delft Pradeshiya Sabha.

NANATTAN  PRADESHIYA  SABHA
Declaration of Names and Details of Roads
IN terms of Section 24 of Pradeshiya Sabha Act, No. 15 of 1987 as per the Decision (administrative order) No. 65 dated
26.07.2016 of Nanattan Pradeshiya Sabha in Mannar District, by virtue of powers vested in Nanattan Pradeshiya Sabha as
per Pradeshiya Sabha Act, Roads under mentioned Schedule published as the Roads belong to Nanattan Pradeshiya Sabha.
It is hereby noticed that in terms of Section 24(2) of Pradeshiya Sabha Act, No. 15 of 1987 if anyone is to be the
owner of the land of the Roads of which are identified by Pradeshiya Sabha shall raise his or her objections to me with the
provable documents within one month from the date of this notice published in the Gazette or institute action in the
appropriate court within three months from the date of this notice published Gazette notice with one month prior notice to
Pradeshiya Sabha to establish his or her ownership.
S. L
OGESW ARAM,
Secretary,
Nanattan Pradeshiya Sabha,
Nanattan.

V ALIKAMAM   EAST   PRADESHIYA   SABHA   PUTTUR
Declaration of Names and Details of Roads
IN terms of Section 24 of Pradeshiya Sabha Act, No. 15 of 1987 as per the decision (administrative order) No. 07 dated 05.07.2016 of Valikamam East Pradeshiya Sabha
in Jaffna District, by virtue of powers vested in Valikamam East Pradeshiya Sabha as per Pradeshiya Sabha Act, roads under mentioned Schedule published as the
roads belong to Valikamam East Pradshiya Sabha.
 It is hereby noticed that in terms of Section 24(2) Pradeshiya Sabha Act, No.15 of 1987 if anyone is to be the owner of the land  of the roads of which are
identified by Pradeshiya  Sabha shall  raise  his or her objections to me with the provable documents within three months from the date of this notice published
Gazette notice with one month prior notice to Pradeshiya Sabha to establish his or her ownership.
Secretary,
Valikamam East Pradeshiya Sabha.

Declaration of Names and Details of Roads
IN terms of Section 24 of Pradeshiya Sabha Act, No. 15 of 1987 as per the decision (administrative order) No. (NP/14/42(02)/mn.com/june/2016/02) dated 15.06.2016
of Mannar Pradeshiya Sabha in Mannar district, by virtue of powers vested in Mannar Pradeshiya Sabha as per Pradeshiya Sabha Act, roads under mentioned
schedule published as the roads belong to Mannar Pradeshiya Sabha.
It is hereby noticed that in terms of Section 24(2) of Pradeshiya Sabha Act, No. 15 of 1987 if anyone is to be the owner of the land of the roads of which
are identified by Pradeshiya Sabha shall raise his or her objections to me with the provable documents within one month from the date of this notice published in
the Gazette or institute action in the appropriate court within three months from the date of this notice published Gazette notice with one month prior notice to
Pradeshiya Sabha to establish his or her ownership.
R. THAYAPARAN,
